 uttarakhand ke chunavi itihaas main gangotri seat se jis bhi party kaa ummidavaar jeeta, pradesh main usee dal kii sarkaar bani
 In such a situation, a saying has become prevalent here that the person who won the Gangotri seat will retain power
 siyasat ke is sanyog ko dharm guru patit paavani maa ganga kii aseem krupa qaraar dete hai
 Whether it is a coincidence or a miracle regarding this seat of Uttarkashi district, the reality is that whichever party candidate from Uttarkashi has won its own government in the state
 ab yah sanyog gangotri vidhansabha seat se jud gaya he, jo ki uttarakhand banane ke baad uttarkashi jile kii vidhansabha seat main parivartit ho gaya
 After the formation of Uttarakhand state in the year 2000, Uttarkashi assembly was divided into four assembly seats in Jaunsar, Tehri, Purola, Yamunotri and Gangotri due to delimitation of assembly seats
 varsh 2002 main rajya main hue pehle chunaav main congress ke vijaypal sajwan congress se jeet kar vidhansabha main pahunche, varsh 2012 main dobaaraa phir congress ke vijaypal ke jeetne par pradesh main unheen kii party congress kii sarkaar bani
 Now it will be interesting to see in the upcoming assembly elections 2017, how long u will remain intact
 uttarkashi ke saath 60 saalon se judaa he mythkauttarkashi kii is seat ke saath yah myth judaa rahaa
 In 1958, Ramchandra Uniyal of Congress became the MLA from Uttarkashi seat of Tehri district, which was part of UP, then the Congress government was formed in the state
 iske baad teen baar congress ke krishna singh vidhayak bane, to pradesh main teenon baar congress kii sarkaar bani
 Congress leader Baldev Singh Arya became MLA here when Uttarkashi assembly seat was declared for Scheduled Caste in 1974, even then Congress government was formed in the state
 vahiin apatkaal ke baad raajnneetik uthal-puthal ke samay janata party asttiv main ai
 At that time, Janta Party's Himachal Lal Juwatha won the elections and the Janata Party government was formed in the state
 aise main uttarkashi seat se jude is myth ko banaae rakhane ke liye bijepi or congress donon dalon ne hi gangotri vidhansabha par hameshaa apni puri takat jhonki he
 This time it will also be a miracle? Given this combination of Gangotri assembly seat, Congress is going to play its seat in the assembly elections this time too, on the other hand, BJP has also fielded its strongest candidate Gopal Rawat
 
 gopal ravat isse pehle bhi chunaav jeet kar bhaajapa ko satta sukh dilaa chuke hai
 Therefore, both the party as well as the common people are excited about the result of the electoral duel in Gangotri seat
 ab dekhne he ki saal 1958 se lekar ab tak jis seat ne party kaa bhagya tay kiya, kya vah is baar bhi itihaas doharaa paaegaa
 
 
 If you have gone against your family and married to your will and you are risking your life, then you can take protection
 supreme court ke edwocket upendra mishra kaa kahana he ki har naagarik kii jivan kii raksha karnaa sarkaar kaa daayitv he
 As far as marriage is concerned, a girl who has completed the age of 18 years and a boy who has completed the age of 21 years can marry on their own
 isamen jati koi baadha nahin banati he
 The law allows it fully
 supreme court ke edwocket upendra mishra ne bataaya ki agar koi apane parijanon ke khilaaf jaakar shaadi karata he or usko apni or apane jivan saathi kii jaan kaa khatra he, to vah ilaake ke police adheekshak se suraksha kii maang kar saktaa he
 He said that if the police refuse to give protection, then such couples can go directly to the High Court under Article 226 of the Constitution and directly to the Supreme Court under Article 32
 edwocket upendra mishra ke mutabik samvidhan ke anuchhed 226 ke tahat hoicourt or anuchhed 32 ke tahat supreme court aise maamle ko sunne ke liye baadhya he
 Under Article 21 of the Constitution, every citizen has got the fundamental right to live life
 agar uske is moulik adhikaar kaa hanan hota he, to supreme court isaki raksha karne ke liye baadhya he
 He told that if a couple goes to the Supreme Court or High Court stating their life as a threat, the courts can order the police and the government to provide protection to the couple
 adaalat ke aadesh ke baad police ko navadanpati ko suraksha muhaiyaa karaani hi hogi

 iske baad se sakshi or unke pati ajitesh kumaar apni jaan ko khatra bataa rahe hai
 In a special conversation with Aaj Tak, both said that they are being chased and they are in danger of life
 sakshi ne bataaya ki jab hamane bareli ke police adheekshak se suraksha dene kii guhaar lagaai, to unhone saaf manaa kar diya
 He also said that he cannot provide any kind of security without a court order
 iske baad sakshi or unke pati ajitesh kumaar ne elahabaad hoicourt main yachika daakhil kar suraksha kii maang kii he

 The ruling Aam Aadmi Party (AAP) in Delhi said on Monday that the Modi government was 'as bad' as the bad Congress-led UPA government
 aap kii rashtriya parishad kii baithak main prastaav paarit kar bhartiya janata party (bijepi) kii 'paidaa kii ja rahi ashishnutaa' kii ranneeti ko 'bharat ke vichaar ke liye gambhir khatra' bataaya gaya he
 The AAP said that in 2014 the people of the country had replaced the most corrupt government of the country with the hope of 'development and good governance'
 lekin, beete 18 maheene main yah vikalp, bijepi netritv vaala endie, utana hi bura sabit hua he
 ' prastaav main kaha gaya he ki bhrashtachar centre sarkaar main har str par vyaapt he
 The rate of economic growth is sluggish
 rojgaar kaa srijan na ke baraabar he

 aap ne kaha he, 'rajnatik rup se bijepi apane ateet ke anuroop hi rahi

 ' prastaav main kaha gaya he, 'bijepi kaa vaastavik agenda ashishnutaa he or rajnatik laabh ke liye samaaj ko baantnaa he
 ' aap ne kaha he ki is 'paidaa kii gai ashishnutaa' ko logon ne nakaar diya he, pehle dilli main or phir bihar main
 But 'bjp's consistent attempt to make it the focal point of its political strategy is a serious threat to India's idea
 ' The AAP has said that it believes that communal and corrupt forces are the main threat to Indian society and the party will oppose them politically
 ' vidhayak sarita singh ke prastaav par aap kii rashtriya parishad ne teen prastaav paarit kiye
 The comments isamen kaha gaya he ki bhrashtachar ke khilaaf andolan se nikalakar aam aadmi party banane tak kaa yah safar kaaphi seekhney vaala rahaa he
 The AAP also accused the Modi government of weakening the federal structure
 aap ne kaha he, 'sahyogi sanghavaad ke bajaae rajyapalon or up-rajyapalon kii madad se gaiyr endie sarkaron ko nishane par liya ja rahaa he
 The party has said that it will create public opinion against this dictatorial attitude of the Modi government towards non-nda governments
